***bewaren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewaren.html>bewaren</a> (2330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewaren.html>bewaren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">biwaron</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">beware</i>.
</p>

</p>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behouden.html>behouden</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guard, to watch <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeden.html>behoeden</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behouden.html>behouden</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewaken.html>bewaken</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewegen.html>bewegen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewegen.html>bewegen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sometimes reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to be in motion

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to cause to be in motion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:benen.html>benen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bewegen.html>bewegen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>move</b> my <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:budge.html>budge</a>, to motivate, to spur, to induce

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a> (1482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewegen.html>bewegen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewegingen.html>bewegingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweginkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>movement, motion <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of physically moving</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schijnbare.html>schijnbare</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zon.html>zon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>langs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemel.html>hemel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevolg.html>gevolg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:draaiing.html>draaiing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>Aarde</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The apparent <b>motion</b> of the sun across the sky <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a consequence of the rotation of the Earth.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>physical activity, exercise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dokter.html>dokter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezegd.html>gezegd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weinig.html>weinig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The doctor <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> get enough <b>exercise</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***beweren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beweren.html>beweren</a> (4646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A merger of two verbs:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beweren.html>beweren</a></i>, an eastern variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewaren.html>bewaren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to prove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">waer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">true</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i>). Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.</li>
<li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beweren.html>beweren</a></i>, a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewaren.html>bewaren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to uphold, to stand one's ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewaren.html>bewaren</a></i>). Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a></i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beweren.html>beweren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to claim, to assert, to allege</li></ol>

***bewijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewijs.html>bewijs</a> (782)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewijs.html>bewijs</a></i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewijzen.html>bewijzen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewijs.html>bewijs</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewijzen.html>bewijzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewijsje.html>bewijsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>proof</li>
<li>evidence</li>
<li>the totality of proof and/or evidence used to make a case; argumentation
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewijsvoering.html>bewijsvoering</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>attesting document, permit</li>
<li>licence, permit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">document allowing one to use certain vehicles</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brevet.html>brevet</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>ticket, pass entitling one to use, admission or possession</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> legal apportionment of an inheritance</li></ol>

***bezem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezem.html>bezem</a> (9655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besem</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*besemo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*besmō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">besom</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Besen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bezetten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezetten.html>bezetten</a> (13215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besetten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bisetten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bisatjaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezetten.html>bezetten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to occupy, to fill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bezet.html>bezet</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> that seat <b><a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a></b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to occupy (forcefully with military personnel), to conquer</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zicht.html>zicht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-igen</i>, replacing earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bezichten</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to behold</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sightsee, to view
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steen.html>steen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rosette.html>Rosette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bezichtigd.html>bezichtigd</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> British Museum in <a href = vnd.unilang:londen.html>Londen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a> 1802 <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewaard.html>bewaard</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:rosetta.html>Rosetta</a> stone can be <b>viewed</b> at the British Museum in London, where it <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> kept ever since 1802.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bisian</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bisehwaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look, besee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a></i>. ***bezig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a> (482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēsich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bisig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bisīg</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>beziger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bezigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>busy, occupied
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He can not talk right now. He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>busy</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a>

***bezighouden.html

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i>.

***bezitten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezitten.html>bezitten</a> (4819)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besitten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">besitten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bisitjaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sit near, sit among</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezitten.html>bezitten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to own, to possess</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although verbs with be- are generally transitive, the passive construction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually avoided for similar reasons as in English as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bezeten.html>bezeten</a></i> refers to demonic possession. A construction with <i>in <a href = vnd.unilang:bezit.html>bezit</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preferred:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijf.html>bedrijf</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bezit.html>bezit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">The company owns this <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>in <a href = vnd.unilang:bezit.html>bezit</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijf.html>bedrijf</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>in the possession</i> of the company.</span></div></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezitting.html>bezitting</a> (49895)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besittinge</i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bezoedelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezoedelen.html>bezoedelen</a> (23224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">besudeln</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezoedelen.html>bezoedelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stain, to besmirch, to <a href = vnd.unilang:sully.html>sully</a></li></ol>
